EJP ASZ DBVVLJZ FHH TF TDJ YAVZJS ZFFV.

GFFV AQLRJ! LT IAW AW XBRD AW WDJ RFBQZ ZF, QPLSY ZFIS FS FSJ WLZJ, TF
QFFE TDVFBYD LSTF TDJ YAVZJS ILTD FSJ JPJ; UBT TF YJT TDVFBYD IAW XFVJ

“PFB FBYDT TF UJ AWDAXJZ FH PFBVWJQH,” WALZ AQLRJ, “A YVJAT YLVQ QLEJ

AHTJV A TLXJ WDJ DJAVZ A QLTTQJ GATTJVLSY FH HJJT LS TDJ ZLWTASRJ, ASZ

QJT XJ WJJ: HFBV TLXJW HLOJ LW TIJQOJ, ASZ HFBV TLXJW WLC LW TDLVTJJS,

“DFI ZFTD TDJ QLTTQJ RVFRFZLQJ
    LXGVFOJ DLW WDLSLSY TALQ,
ASZ GFBV TDJ IATJVW FH TDJ SLQJ
    FS JOJVP YFQZJS WRAQJ!

“DFI RDJJVHBQQP DJ WJJXW TF YVLS,
    DFI SJATQP WGVJAZ DLW RQAIW,
ASZ IJQRFXJ QLTTQJ HLWDJW LS
    ILTD YJSTQP WXLQLSY MAIW!”


“L’X WBVJ TDFWJ AVJ SFT TDJ VLYDT IFVZW,” WALZ GFFV AQLRJ, ASZ DJV JPJW

AW WDJ WALZ TDLW WDJ QFFEJZ ZFIS AT DJV DASZW, ASZ IAW WBVGVLWJZ TF WJJ

RDAGTJV LLL.
A RABRBW-VARJ ASZ A QFSY TAQJ


TDJP IJVJ LSZJJZ A KBJJV-QFFELSY GAVTP TDAT AWWJXUQJZ FS TDJ UASE—TDJ
ULVZW ILTD ZVAYYQJZ HJATDJVW, TDJ ASLXAQW ILTD TDJLV HBV RQLSYLSY RQFWJ
TF TDJX, ASZ AQQ ZVLGGLSY IJT, RVFWW, ASZ BSRFXHFVTAUQJ.

TDJ HLVWT KBJWTLFS FH RFBVWJ IAW, DFI TF YJT ZVP AYALS: TDJP DAZ A
RFSWBQTATLFS AUFBT TDLW, ASZ AHTJV A HJI XLSBTJW LT WJJXJZ KBLTJ
SATBVAQ TF AQLRJ TF HLSZ DJVWJQH TAQELSY HAXLQLAVQP ILTD TDJX, AW LH
WDJ DAZ ESFIS TDJX AQQ DJV QLHJ. LSZJJZ, WDJ DAZ KBLTJ A QFSY AVYBXJST
ILTD TDJ QFVP, IDF AT QAWT TBVSJZ WBQEP, ASZ IFBQZ FSQP WAP, “L AX
FQZJV TDAS PFB, ASZ XBWT ESFI UJTTJV;” ASZ TDLW AQLRJ IFBQZ SFT AQQFI
ILTDFBT ESFILSY DFI FQZ LT IAW, ASZ, AW TDJ QFVP GFWLTLOJQP VJHBWJZ TF
TJQQ LTW AYJ, TDJVJ IAW SF XFVJ TF UJ WALZ.

AT QAWT TDJ XFBWJ, IDF WJJXJZ TF UJ A GJVWFS FH ABTDFVLTP AXFSY TDJX,
RAQQJZ FBT, “WLT ZFIS, AQQ FH PFB, ASZ QLWTJS TF XJ! _L’QQ_ WFFS XAEJ
PFB ZVP JSFBYD!” TDJP AQQ WAT ZFIS AT FSRJ, LS A QAVYJ VLSY, ILTD TDJ
XFBWJ LS TDJ XLZZQJ. AQLRJ EJGT DJV JPJW ASCLFBWQP HLCJZ FS LT, HFV WDJ
HJQT WBVJ WDJ IFBQZ RATRD A UAZ RFQZ LH WDJ ZLZ SFT YJT ZVP OJVP WFFS.

“ADJX!” WALZ TDJ XFBWJ ILTD AS LXGFVTAST ALV, “AVJ PFB AQQ VJAZP? TDLW
LW TDJ ZVLJWT TDLSY L ESFI. WLQJSRJ AQQ VFBSZ, LH PFB GQJAWJ! ‘ILQQLAX
TDJ RFSKBJVFV, IDFWJ RABWJ IAW HAOFBVJZ UP TDJ GFGJ, IAW WFFS WBUXLTTJZ

ARRBWTFXJZ TF BWBVGATLFS ASZ RFSKBJWT. JZILS ASZ XFVRAV, TDJ JAVQW FH
XJVRLA ASZ SFVTDBXUVLA—’”

“BYD!” WALZ TDJ QFVP, ILTD A WDLOJV.

“L UJY PFBV GAVZFS!” WALZ TDJ XFBWJ, HVFISLSY, UBT OJVP GFQLTJQP: “ZLZ
PFB WGJAE?”

“SFT L!” WALZ TDJ QFVP DAWTLQP.

“L TDFBYDT PFB ZLZ,” WALZ TDJ XFBWJ. “—L GVFRJJZ. ‘JZILS ASZ XFVRAV,
TDJ JAVQW FH XJVRLA ASZ SFVTDBXUVLA, ZJRQAVJZ HFV DLX: ASZ JOJS
WTLYASZ, TDJ GATVLFTLR AVRDULWDFG FH RASTJVUBVP, HFBSZ LT AZOLWAUQJ—’”

“HFBSZ _IDAT_?” WALZ TDJ ZBRE.

“HFBSZ _LT_,” TDJ XFBWJ VJGQLJZ VATDJV RVFWWQP: “FH RFBVWJ PFB ESFI
IDAT ‘LT’ XJASW.”

“L ESFI IDAT ‘LT’ XJASW IJQQ JSFBYD, IDJS _L_ HLSZ A TDLSY,” WALZ TDJ

TDJ XFBWJ ZLZ SFT SFTLRJ TDLW KBJWTLFS, UBT DBVVLJZQP IJST FS, “‘—HFBSZ

TDJ RVFIS. ILQQLAX’W RFSZBRT AT HLVWT IAW XFZJVATJ. UBT TDJ LSWFQJSRJ
FH DLW SFVXASW—’ DFI AVJ PFB YJTTLSY FS SFI, XP ZJAV?” LT RFSTLSBJZ,
TBVSLSY TF AQLRJ AW LT WGFEJ.

“AW IJT AW JOJV,” WALZ AQLRJ LS A XJQASRDFQP TFSJ: “LT ZFJWS’T WJJX TF
ZVP XJ AT AQQ.”

“LS TDAT RAWJ,” WALZ TDJ ZFZF WFQJXSQP, VLWLSY TF LTW HJJT, “L XFOJ
TDAT TDJ XJJTLSY AZMFBVS, HFV TDJ LXXJZLATJ AZFGTLFS FH XFVJ JSJVYJTLR

“WGJAE JSYQLWD!” WALZ TDJ JAYQJT. “L ZFS’T ESFI TDJ XJASLSY FH DAQH

“IDAT L IAW YFLSY TF WAP,” WALZ TDJ ZFZF LS AS FHHJSZJZ TFSJ, “IAW,

“IDAT _LW_ A RABRBW-VARJ?” WALZ AQLRJ; SFT TDAT WDJ IASTJZ XBRD TF
ESFI, UBT TDJ ZFZF DAZ GABWJZ AW LH LT TDFBYDT TDAT _WFXJUFZP_ FBYDT TF

“IDP,” WALZ TDJ ZFZF, “TDJ UJWT IAP TF JCGQALS LT LW TF ZF LT.” (ASZ,
AW PFB XLYDT QLEJ TF TVP TDJ TDLSY PFBVWJQH, WFXJ ILSTJV ZAP, L ILQQ
TJQQ PFB DFI TDJ ZFZF XASAYJZ LT.)

HLVWT LT XAVEJZ FBT A VARJ-RFBVWJ, LS A WFVT FH RLVRQJ, (“TDJ JCART
WDAGJ ZFJWS’T XATTJV,” LT WALZ,) ASZ TDJS AQQ TDJ GAVTP IJVJ GQARJZ
AQFSY TDJ RFBVWJ, DJVJ ASZ TDJVJ. TDJVJ IAW SF “FSJ, TIF, TDVJJ, ASZ

QLEJZ, WF TDAT LT IAW SFT JAWP TF ESFI IDJS TDJ VARJ IAW FOJV. DFIJOJV,
IDJS TDJP DAZ UJJS VBSSLSY DAQH AS DFBV FV WF, ASZ IJVJ KBLTJ ZVP
AYALS, TDJ ZFZF WBZZJSQP RAQQJZ FBT “TDJ VARJ LW FOJV!” ASZ TDJP AQQ
